let user_country_code = "";
(function () {
	let country_list = country_and_states["country"];
	let states_list = country_and_states["states"];
	let state_code_id = document.getElementsByName("stateProv")[0];
	function create_states_dropdown(code) {
		let text_box = '<input type="text" class="input-text" id="stateProv">';

		let country_code = document.getElementsByName("country")[0].value;
		console.log(country_code);
		let state_code_id_state = document.getElementsByName("stateProv")[0];
		let states = states_list[country_code];
		let option = "";
		if (!states) {
			state_code_id_state.innerHTML = '<option value="">State/Province</>';
			return;
		}
		if (states.length > 0) {
			option = '<select id="state">\n<option value="">State/Province</>';
			for (let i = 0; i < states.length; i++) {
				option +=
					'<option value="' +
					states[i].regionCode +
					'">' +
					states[i].regionDisplayName +
					"</option>";
			}
			option += "</select>";
		} else {
			option = text_box;
		}
		state_code_id_state.innerHTML = option;
	}
	const country_select = document.getElementsByName("country")[0];
	country_select.addEventListener("change", create_states_dropdown);
	country_select.addEventListener("onfocus", create_states_dropdown);
	country_select.addEventListener("onblur", create_states_dropdown);
	//create_states_dropdown();

	window.addEventListener("load", create_states_dropdown);
})();
